or the &#8220;Company&#8221;) (NYSE&#58;FDS) (NASDAQ&#58;FDS), a global provider of integrated financial information, analytical applications, and industry-leading service, today announced results for its third quarter ended May&#160;31, 2021. </font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#004988;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">Third Quarter Fiscal 2021 Highlights</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div style="padding-left:27.35pt;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#8226;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;padding-left:14.85pt">Revenue increased 6.8%, or $25.5 million, to $399.6 million compared with $374.1 million for the same period in fiscal 2020. The increase is primarily due to higher sales of analytics and content and technology solutions (CTS).</font><font style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%"> Organic revenues grew 5.9%</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%"> to $397.4 million during the third quarter of fiscal 2021 from the prior year period. </font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div style="margin-bottom:10pt;padding-left:27.35pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">&#8226;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%;padding-left:14.85pt">Annual Subscription Value (ASV) plus professional services was $1.6 billion at May&#160;31, 2021, compared with $1.5 billion at May&#160;31, 2020. The organic ASV plus professional services growth rate, which excludes the effects of acquisitions and dispositions completed within the last 12 months, and foreign currency movements, was 5.8%. The primary contributors to this growth were higher sales of research and analytics solutions. Please see the &#8220;ASV + Professional Services&#8221; section of this press release for details.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:10pt;padding-left:27.35pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">&#8226;</font><font style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%;padding-left:14.85pt">Operating margin decreased to 29.5% compared with 32.5% for the same period last year. Adjusted operating margin decreased to </font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">31.6% compared with 35.5% in the prior year period primarily as a result of higher spending for the Company's multi-year investment plan as well as increased performance based compensation reflecting the acceleration in ASV.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:10pt;padding-left:27.35pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">&#8226;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%;padding-left:14.85pt">Diluted earnings per share (EPS) decreased 0.4% to $2.62 compared with $2.63 for the same period in fiscal 2020. Adjusted diluted EPS fell 4.9% to $2.72 compared with </font><font style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">$2.86 i</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">n the prior year period primarily due to higher operating expenses partially offset by higher revenues. </font></div><div style="margin-bottom:10pt;padding-left:27.35pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">&#8226;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%;padding-left:14.85pt">The Company&#8217;s effective tax rate for the third quarter decreased to 11.9% compared with 15.0% a year ago, primarily due to lower operating income and a tax benefit related to finalizing prior year's tax returns compared with a tax expense for the three months ended May&#160;31, 2020. </font></div><div style="margin-bottom:10pt;padding-left:27.35pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">&#8226;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%;padding-left:14.85pt">The Company increased its quarterly dividend by 6.5% to $0.82, marking the twenty-second consecutive year of dividend increases.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:10pt;padding-left:27.35pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">&#8226;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%;padding-left:14.85pt">FactSet has increased its organic ASV plus professional services outlook to be in the range of $85 million to $95 million. FactSet reaffirms other metrics of its annual outlook for fiscal 2021. Please see the &#8220;Annual Business Outlook&#8221; section of this press release for details.</font></div><div style="padding-left:27.35pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-18pt"><font><br></font></div><div style="margin-bottom:10pt;text-align:justify"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">&#8220;I&#8217;m pleased with the acceleration in our top line and proud of our record of returning value to our shareholders every year since we became a public company 25 years ago,&#8221; said Phil Snow, CEO, FactSet. &#8220;Demand for our open content and analytics platform continues to fuel our growth as clients pursue their own digital transformations. We believe that the next generation of digital solutions we are building for the financial community will enable us to grow faster.&#8221;</font></div><div growth this quarter. In line with our operating plan, we are investing in both technology and talent, while remaining disciplined on costs and returns,&#8221; said Helen Shan, CFO and Chief Revenue Officer (CRO), FactSet. &#8220;We are confident in our ability to convert our healthy fourth quarter pipeline and are on track to finish this year on a solid note.&#8221;</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div style="margin-bottom:10pt;text-align:justify"><font style="color:#004988;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">Annual Subscription Value (ASV) + Professional Services </font></div><div style="margin-bottom:10pt;text-align:justify"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">ASV at any given point in time represents the forward-looking revenues for the next twelve months from all subscription services currently supplied to clients. Professional services are revenues derived from project-based consulting and implementation.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:10pt;text-align:justify"><font style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">ASV plus professional services was $1,617 million at May&#160;31, 2021. Organic ASV plus professional services was $1,612 million at May&#160;31, 2021, up $88.6 million from the prior year at a growth rate of 5.8%. Organic ASV, which excludes the effects of acquisitions and dispositions </font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">completed within the last 12 months,</font><font style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%"> and foreign currency movements, plus professional services, increased $19.3 million over the last three months. </font></div><div style="text-align:justify"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">Buy-side and sell-side ASV growth rates for the third quarter of fiscal 2021 were 5.6% and 8.0%, respectively. Buy-side clients that </font><font style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">primarily includes portfolio managers, analysts, traders and wealth managers, </font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">accounted for approximately 84%</font><font style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%"> of organic ASV while the remainder was derived from sell-side firms that perform mergers and acquisitions advisory work, capital markets services, and equity research. Supplementary tables covering organic buy-side and sell-side ASV growth rates may be found on the last page of this press release. </font></div><div style="text-align:justify"><font><br></font></div><div style="text-align:justify"><font style="color:#004988;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">Segment Revenue and ASV</font></div><div style="text-align:justify"><font><br></font></div><div style="margin-bottom:10pt;text-align:justify"><font style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">ASV from the Americas region was $993.4 million compared with ASV in the prior year period of $931.5 million. Organic ASV increased 6.0% to $987.8 million. </font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">Americas revenues for the quarter increased to $253.8 million compared with $238.5 million in the third quarter last year. Excluding the effects of acquisitions and dispositions completed in the last 12 months, the Americas region organic revenue growth rate was 5.8%. </font></div><div style="height:72pt;position:relative;width:100%"><div style="bottom:0;position:absolute;width:100%"><div style="margin-bottom:10pt;text-align:right"><font style="color:#afafaf;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:7pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">2</font></div><div style="padding-right:18pt"><font style="color:#dcdcdc;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:6pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;</font></div></div></div><hr style="page-break-after:always"><div style="min-height:86.4pt;width:100%"><div style="margin-bottom:10pt"><font><br></font></div><div style="margin-bottom:10pt"><font style="color:#afafaf;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:8pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">News Release </font><font style="color:#98ca3c;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:8pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">I</font><font style="color:#afafaf;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:8pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%"> For Immediate Release</font></div></div><div style="margin-bottom:10pt;text-align:justify"><font style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">ASV from the EMEA region was $436.4 million compared with ASV in the prior year period of $411.9 million. Organic ASV increased 4.7% to $435.9 million. </font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">EMEA revenues were $106.8 million compared with $100.4 million in the third quarter of fiscal 2020. Excluding the effects of acquisitions and dispositions completed in the last 12 months and foreign currency impacts, the EMEA region organic revenue growth rate was 4.5%. </font></div><div style="margin-bottom:10pt;text-align:justify"><font style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">ASV from the Asia Pacific region was $163.4 million compared with ASV in the prior year period of $150.4 million. Organic ASV increased 9.1% to $164.4 million. Asia Pacific revenues were $38.9 million compared with $35.2 million in the third quarter of fiscal 2020. </font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">Excluding the effects of acquisitions and dispositions completed in the last 12 months and foreign currency impacts, the Asia Pacific region organic revenue growth rate was 11.0%. </font></div><div style="margin-bottom:10pt;text-align:justify"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">Segment ASV does not include professional services, which totaled $23.9 million at May&#160;31, 2021.</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#004988;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">Operational Highlights &#8211; Third Quarter Fiscal 2021</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div style="margin-bottom:10pt;padding-left:27pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">&#9702;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%;padding-left:14.81pt">Client count as of May&#160;31, 2021 was 6,172, a net increase of 69 clients in the past three months, primarily driven by an increase in wealth management and corporate clients as well as third party data providers. The count includes clients with ASV of $10,000 and above.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:10pt;padding-left:27pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">&#9702;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%;padding-left:14.81pt">User count increased by 1,649 to 155,004 in the past three months, primarily driven by an increase in research, wealth and corporate solutions users.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:10pt;padding-left:27pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">&#9702;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%;padding-left:14.81pt">Annual ASV retention was greater than 95%. When expressed as a percentage of clients, annual retention improved to 91%, year over year. </font></div><div style="margin-bottom:10pt;padding-left:27pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">&#9702;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%;padding-left:14.81pt">Employee count was 10,713 as of May&#160;31, 2021, up 6.4% over the last twelve months. Excluding the Truvalue Labs acquisition, headcount grew by 6.1%, primarily driven by increased hiring in the Company's content and product development organizations.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:10pt;padding-left:27pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">&#9702;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%;padding-left:14.81pt">Net cash provided by operating activities decreased to $140.3 million compared with $151.0 million for the third quarter of 2020. Quarterly free cash flow decreased to $121.7 million compared with $139.9 million a year ago, a decrease of 13.1%, primarily due to higher capital expenditures and the timing of certain tax items.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:10pt;padding-left:27pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">&#9702;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%;padding-left:14.81pt">Capital expenditures increased to $18.7 million, compared with $11.0 million a year ago, primarily due to higher investment in internal use software. </font></div><div style="margin-bottom:10pt;padding-left:27pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">&#9702;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%;padding-left:14.81pt">A quarterly dividend of $31.0 million, or $0.82 per share, was paid on June&#160;17, 2021, to holders of record of FactSet&#8217;s common stock at the close of business on May&#160;31, 2021. The $0.05 per share or 6.5% increase to $0.82 marked the twenty-second consecutive year the Company has increased dividends, highlighting its continued commitment to returning value to shareholders.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:10pt;padding-left:27pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">&#9702;</font><font style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%;padding-left:14.81pt">FactSet appointed Executive Vice President Helen Shan to the role of CRO. In this role, she is responsible for all aspects of FactSet&#8217;s revenue performance, including the management of its global Sales organization and the execution of its go-to-market strategy. Shan will continue to serve as CFO until a successor is named.</font></div><div style="padding-left:27pt;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:112%">&#9702;</font><font style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:112%;padding-left:14.11pt">FactSet was named the Best Alternative Data Provider, Best ESG Data Provider, and Best Overall Data or Service Provider for 2021 at the Waters Technology Inside Market Data and Inside Reference Data Awards. The company also won most innovative ESG initiative at the A-Team Innovation Awards and ESG data provider of the year at the Sustainable Investment Awards 2021.</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div style="margin-bottom:10pt;padding-left:27pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%">&#9702;</font><font style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:133%;padding-left:14.81pt">FactSet and the Tokyo Stock Exchange (TSE) announced plans to develop a new series of co-branded thematic indices targeting Japanese stocks.
